<p>The <b>Academy Award for Best Actress</b> is an award presented annually by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_of_Motion_Picture_Arts_and_Sciences" title="Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences">Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences</a> (AMPAS). It has been awarded since the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Academy_Awards" title="1st Academy Awards">1st Academy Awards</a> to an actress who has delivered an outstanding performance in a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leading_actor" title="Leading actor">leading</a> role in a film released that year. The award is traditionally presented by the previous year's <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actor" title="Academy Award for Best Actor">Best Actor</a> winner.
</p><p>The Best Actress award has been presented 97 times, to 79 actresses. The first winner was <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janet_Gaynor" title="Janet Gaynor">Janet Gaynor</a> for her roles in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/7th_Heaven_(1927_film)" title="7th Heaven (1927 film)">7th Heaven</a></i>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Street_Angel_(1928_film)" title="Street Angel (1928 film)">Street Angel</a></i>, and <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sunrise:_A_Song_of_Two_Humans" title="Sunrise: A Song of Two Humans">Sunrise: A Song of Two Humans</a></i>. The most recent winner is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Stone" title="Emma Stone">Emma Stone</a> for her role in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poor_Things_(film)" title="Poor Things (film)">Poor Things</a></i> (2023); she had previously won the award for her role in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/La_La_Land" title="La La Land">La La Land</a></i> (2016). The record for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_actors_with_two_or_more_Academy_Awards_in_acting_categories" title="List of actors with two or more Academy Awards in acting categories">most wins</a> is four, held by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Katharine_Hepburn" title="Katharine Hepburn">Katharine Hepburn</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frances_McDormand" title="Frances McDormand">Frances McDormand</a> has won thrice, while thirteen other actresses have won the award twice. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Meryl_Streep" title="Meryl Streep">Meryl Streep</a> has received the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_actors_with_three_or_more_Academy_Award_nominations_in_acting_categories" class="mw-redirect" title="List of actors with three or more Academy Award nominations in acting categories">most nominations</a> in this category—seventeen—and has won twice. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deborah_Kerr" title="Deborah Kerr">Deborah Kerr</a> holds the record in this category for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_actors_with_three_or_more_Academy_Award_nominations_in_acting_categories#Most_nominations_by_category_(actor)" class="mw-redirect" title="List of actors with three or more Academy Award nominations in acting categories">most nominations (six) without a win</a>—albeit in 1993, she was an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Honorary_Award#1990s" title="Academy Honorary Award">Honorary Oscar recipient</a>. At the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/41st_Academy_Awards" title="41st Academy Awards">41st Academy Awards</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbra_Streisand" title="Barbra Streisand">Barbra Streisand</a> and Katharine Hepburn received the same number of votes and thus tied for Best Actress (the only time this has occurred). <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Italian_Academy_Award_winners_and_nominees" title="List of Italian Academy Award winners and nominees">Italian actress</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sophia_Loren" title="Sophia Loren">Sophia Loren</a> became the first actor, in any category, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_actors_nominated_for_Academy_Awards_for_non-English_performances" title="List of actors nominated for Academy Awards for non-English performances">to win for a foreign language performance</a> in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Two_Women" title="Two Women">Two Women</a></i> (1960).
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Nominations_process">Nominations process</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Nominations process"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Nominees are currently determined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Single_transferable_vote" title="Single transferable vote">single transferable vote</a> within the actors branch of AMPAS; winners are selected by a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plurality_(voting)" title="Plurality (voting)">plurality vote</a> from the entire <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Film_industry" title="Film industry">eligible voting members</a> of the Academy.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-1"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> 
</p><p>In the first three years of the awards, actors and actresses were nominated as the best individuals in their categories. At that time, all of their work during the qualifying period (as many as three films, in some cases) was listed after the award.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_history_2-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_history-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Despite this, at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/3rd_Academy_Awards" title="3rd Academy Awards">3rd Academy Awards</a>, held in 1930, only one film was cited in each winner's award regardless of how many they were eligible to be considered for during that span.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The current system, in which an actress is nominated for a specific performance in a single film, was introduced for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/4th_Academy_Awards" title="4th Academy Awards">4th Academy Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_history_2-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_history-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Starting with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/9th_Academy_Awards" title="9th Academy Awards">9th Academy Awards</a>, held in 1937, the category was limited to a maximum five nominations per year.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_history_2-2" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_history-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Winners_and_nominees">Winners and nominees</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Winners and nominees"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>In the following table, the years are listed as per Academy convention, and generally correspond to the year of film release in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Los_Angeles_County" class="mw-redirect" title="Los Angeles County">Los Angeles County</a>; the ceremonies are always held the following year.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> For the first five ceremonies, the eligibility period spanned twelve months, from August 1 to July 31.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_eligibility_5-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_eligibility-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> For the 6th ceremony held in 1934, the eligibility period lasted from August 1, 1932, to December 31, 1933.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_eligibility_5-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_eligibility-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Since the 7th ceremony held in 1935, the period of eligibility became the full previous calendar year from January 1 to December 31.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_eligibility_5-2" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_eligibility-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<table class="wikitable">
<caption>Table key
</caption>
<tbody><tr>
<th scope="row" style="background:#FAEB86;">‡
</th>
<td style="background:#FAEB86;"><b>Indicates the winner</b>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row" style="text-align:center">†
</th>
<td>Indicates <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_posthumous_Academy_Award_winners_and_nominees" title="List of posthumous Academy Award winners and nominees">a posthumous nominee</a>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Films_with_multiple_Leading_Actress_nominations">Films with multiple Leading Actress nominations</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Films with multiple Leading Actress nominations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Winners are in <b>bold</b>.
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/All_About_Eve" title="All About Eve">All About Eve</a></i> (1950) – <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anne_Baxter" title="Anne Baxter">Anne Baxter</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bette_Davis" title="Bette Davis">Bette Davis</a></li>
<li><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suddenly,_Last_Summer_(film)" title="Suddenly, Last Summer (film)">Suddenly, Last Summer</a></i> (1959) – <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Katharine_Hepburn" title="Katharine Hepburn">Katharine Hepburn</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elizabeth_Taylor" title="Elizabeth Taylor">Elizabeth Taylor</a></li>
<li><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Turning_Point_(1977_film)" title="The Turning Point (1977 film)">The Turning Point</a></i> (1977) – <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anne_Bancroft" title="Anne Bancroft">Anne Bancroft</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shirley_MacLaine" title="Shirley MacLaine">Shirley MacLaine</a></li>
<li><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terms_of_Endearment" title="Terms of Endearment">Terms of Endearment</a></i> (1983) – <b>Shirley MacLaine</b> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debra_Winger" title="Debra Winger">Debra Winger</a></li>
<li><i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thelma_%26_Louise" title="Thelma &amp; Louise">Thelma &amp; Louise</a></i> (1991) – <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geena_Davis" title="Geena Davis">Geena Davis</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Susan_Sarandon" title="Susan Sarandon">Susan Sarandon</a></li></ul>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Multiple_character_nominations">Multiple character nominations</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Multiple character nominations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The following were nominated for their portrayals of the same fictional or non-fictional character in separate films (including variations of the original).
</p>
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Billie_Holiday" title="Billie Holiday">Billie Holiday</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lady_Sings_the_Blues_(film)" title="Lady Sings the Blues (film)">Lady Sings the Blues</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diana_Ross" title="Diana Ross">Diana Ross</a>, 1972)</small> &amp; <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_United_States_vs._Billie_Holiday" title="The United States vs. Billie Holiday">The United States vs. Billie Holiday</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andra_Day" title="Andra Day">Andra Day</a>, 2021)</small></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jo_March" class="mw-redirect" title="Jo March">Josephine "Jo" March</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Little_Women_(1994_film)" title="Little Women (1994 film)">Little Women</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winona_Ryder" title="Winona Ryder">Winona Ryder</a>, 1994)</small> &amp; <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Little_Women_(2019_film)" title="Little Women (2019 film)">Little Women</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saoirse_Ronan" title="Saoirse Ronan">Saoirse Ronan</a>, 2019)</small></li>

<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marilyn_Monroe" title="Marilyn Monroe">Marilyn Monroe</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/My_Week_with_Marilyn" title="My Week with Marilyn">My Week with Marilyn</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michelle_Williams_(actress)" title="Michelle Williams (actress)">Michelle Williams</a>, 2011)</small> &amp; <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blonde_(2022_film)" title="Blonde (2022 film)">Blonde</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ana_de_Armas" title="Ana de Armas">Ana de Armas</a>, 2022)</small></li>

<li>Vicki Lester <small>(<span title="Name at birth"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Birth_name#Maiden_and_married_names" title="Birth name">née</a>&nbsp;Esther (Victoria) Blodgett</span>)</small> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Star_Is_Born_(1937_film)" title="A Star Is Born (1937 film)">A Star Is Born</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janet_Gaynor" title="Janet Gaynor">Janet Gaynor</a>, 1937)</small> &amp; <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Star_Is_Born_(1954_film)" title="A Star Is Born (1954 film)">A Star Is Born</a></i> <small>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judy_Garland" title="Judy Garland">Judy Garland</a>, 1954)</small>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notes">Notes</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Notes"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1239549316">.mw-parser-output .refbegin{margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul{margin-left:0}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul>li{margin-left:0;padding-left:3.2em;text-indent:-3.2em}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents ul,.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents ul li{list-style:none}@media(max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .refbegin-hanging-indents>ul>li{padding-left:1.6em;text-indent:-1.6em}}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-columns{margin-top:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-columns ul{margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .refbegin-columns li{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}@media screen{.mw-parser-output .refbegin{font-size:90%}}</style><div class="refbegin" style="">
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1239543626">.mw-parser-output .reflist{margin-bottom:0.5em;list-style-type:decimal}@media screen{.mw-parser-output .reflist{font-size:90%}}.mw-parser-output .reflist .references{font-size:100%;margin-bottom:0;list-style-type:inherit}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-2{column-width:30em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-3{column-width:25em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns{margin-top:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns ol{margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns li{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-alpha{list-style-type:upper-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-roman{list-style-type:upper-roman}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-alpha{list-style-type:lower-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-greek{list-style-type:lower-greek}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-roman{list-style-type:lower-roman}</style><div class="reflist">
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-twentynine-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_ref-twentynine_7-0" aria-label="Jump up" title="Jump up">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The 2nd Academy Awards is unique in being the only occasion where there were no official nominees. Subsequent research by AMPAS has resulted in a list of unofficial or de facto nominees, based on records of which films were evaluated by the judges.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
<dl><dd><b>A</b><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Shearer1"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Shearer1"><b><sup>1</sup></b></a></span> <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Garbo2"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Garbo2"><b><sup>2</sup></b></a></span>&nbsp;: Rules at the time of the first three ceremonies allowed for a performer to receive a single nomination which could honor their work in more than one film. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greta_Garbo" title="Greta Garbo">Greta Garbo</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norma_Shearer" title="Norma Shearer">Norma Shearer</a> were both nominated for two different roles in the same category. Current Academy rules forbid this from happening. No official reason was ever given as to why Shearer won the award for only one of the two films she was listed for.<sup id="cite_ref-Variety_Double_Oscar_Nominations_106-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Variety_Double_Oscar_Nominations-106"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>105<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></dd>
<dd><b>B</b><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Davis"><b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Davis">^</a></b></span>&nbsp;: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bette_Davis" title="Bette Davis">Bette Davis</a>'s performance in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Of_Human_Bondage_(1934_film)" title="Of Human Bondage (1934 film)">Of Human Bondage</a></i> was not nominated for an Oscar.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-107"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>106<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Several influential people at the time campaigned to have her name included on the list, so for that year (and the following year also) the Academy relaxed its rules and allowed a write-in vote.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-108"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>107<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Technically this meant that any performance was eligible to win the award, whether or not the person was an official nominee. While the Academy does not officially recognize this as a nomination for Davis,<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-109"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>108<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-110"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>109<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> it has included her in the list of nominees for the 1935 ceremony on its official website.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscars7_13-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscars7-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></dd>
<dd><b>C</b><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Tie1"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Tie1"><b><sup>1</sup></b></a></span> <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Tie2"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Tie2"><b><sup>2</sup></b></a></span>&nbsp;: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Katharine_Hepburn" title="Katharine Hepburn">Katharine Hepburn</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbra_Streisand" title="Barbra Streisand">Barbra Streisand</a> received the same number of votes, resulting in both actresses receiving the award, according to Academy rules.<sup id="cite_ref-Oscar_tie_111-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-Oscar_tie-111"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>110<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></dd>
<dd><b>D</b><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1041539562"><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_Donnelley"><b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#ref_Donnelley">^</a></b></span>&nbsp;: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elliot_Page" title="Elliot Page">Elliot Page</a> was nominated as Ellen Page, before his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gender_transitioning" class="mw-redirect" title="Gender transitioning">gender transition</a> in 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-elliotpage_112-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress#cite_note-elliotpage-112"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>111<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
